Archiving files

- <span class="s1" style="font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-alternates: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-variant-position: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: normal;"></span>some popular programs for managing backups: Amanda, Bacula, Bareos, Duplicity, BackupPC
- <span class="s1" style="font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-alternates: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-variant-position: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: normal;"></span>we are focusing on cli utilities: cpio, dd, tar

- <span class="s1" style="font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-alternates: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-variant-position: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: normal;"></span>$ cpio —> copy files to and from archives (copy in and out)
- <span class="s1" style="font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-alternates: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-variant-position: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: normal;"></span>$ tar —> an archiving utility for creating tarball

- <span class="s1" style="font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-alternates: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-variant-position: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: normal;"></span>The tar command’s commonly used tarball creation options:

- <span class="s1" style="font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-alternates: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-variant-position: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: normal;"></span>-c, --create —> create a new archive. The backup can be a full or incremental backup, depending on the other selected options.
- <span class="s1" style="font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-alternates: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-variant-position: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: normal;"></span>-u, --update —> only append files newer than copy in archive
- <span class="s1" style="font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-alternates: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-variant-position: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: normal;"></span>-g, --listed-incremental=FILE —> handle new GNU-format incremental backup
- <span class="s1" style="font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-alternates: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-variant-position: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: normal;"></span>-v, --verbose —> verbosely list files processed
- <span class="s1" style="font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-alternates: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-variant-position: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: normal;"></span>-f, --file=ARCHIVE —> use archive file or device ARCHIVE

- <span class="s1" style="font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-alternates: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-variant-position: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: normal;"></span>It is possible to create full backups using tarball snapshot file or .snar with -g option
- <span class="s1" style="font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-alternates: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-variant-position: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: normal;"></span>It is poosible to create incremental backuos using tar
- <span class="s1" style="font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-alternates: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-variant-position: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: normal;"></span>Compressing tar archives is achieved via adding an option to tar as follows:

<table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" class="t1" style="border-collapse: collapse;">

<tbody>

<tr>

<td valign="top" class="td1" style="border-style: solid; border-width: 1px; border-color: rgb(154, 154, 154); padding: 1px 5px;">

Compression Algorithm

</td>

<td valign="top" class="td1" style="border-style: solid; border-width: 1px; border-color: rgb(154, 154, 154); padding: 1px 5px;">

Tar Option

</td>

<td valign="top" class="td1" style="border-style: solid; border-width: 1px; border-color: rgb(154, 154, 154); padding: 1px 5px;">

Tar Filename extension

</td>

<td valign="top" class="td1" style="border-style: solid; border-width: 1px; border-color: rgb(154, 154, 154); padding: 1px 5px;">

Decompression Option

</td>

</tr>

<tr>

<td valign="top" class="td1" style="border-style: solid; border-width: 1px; border-color: rgb(154, 154, 154); padding: 1px 5px;">

gzip

</td>

<td valign="top" class="td1" style="border-style: solid; border-width: 1px; border-color: rgb(154, 154, 154); padding: 1px 5px;">

-z, —gzip

</td>

<td valign="top" class="td1" style="border-style: solid; border-width: 1px; border-color: rgb(154, 154, 154); padding: 1px 5px;">

.tgz or .tar.gz

</td>

<td valign="top" class="td1" style="border-style: solid; border-width: 1px; border-color: rgb(154, 154, 154); padding: 1px 5px;">

-z, —gunzip

</td>

</tr>

<tr>

<td valign="top" class="td1" style="border-style: solid; border-width: 1px; border-color: rgb(154, 154, 154); padding: 1px 5px;">

bzip2

</td>

<td valign="top" class="td1" style="border-style: solid; border-width: 1px; border-color: rgb(154, 154, 154); padding: 1px 5px;">

-j, —bzip2

</td>

<td valign="top" class="td1" style="border-style: solid; border-width: 1px; border-color: rgb(154, 154, 154); padding: 1px 5px;">

.tbz or .tbz2 or .tb2 or .tar.bz2

</td>

<td valign="top" class="td1" style="border-style: solid; border-width: 1px; border-color: rgb(154, 154, 154); padding: 1px 5px;">

-j, —bunzip2

</td>

</tr>

<tr>

<td valign="top" class="td1" style="border-style: solid; border-width: 1px; border-color: rgb(154, 154, 154); padding: 1px 5px;">

xz

</td>

<td valign="top" class="td1" style="border-style: solid; border-width: 1px; border-color: rgb(154, 154, 154); padding: 1px 5px;">

-J, —xz

</td>

<td valign="top" class="td1" style="border-style: solid; border-width: 1px; border-color: rgb(154, 154, 154); padding: 1px 5px;">

.txz or .tar.xz

</td>

<td valign="top" class="td1" style="border-style: solid; border-width: 1px; border-color: rgb(154, 154, 154); padding: 1px 5px;">

-J, —unxz

</td>

</tr>

</tbody>

</table>

- <span class="s1" style="font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-alternates: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-variant-position: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: normal;"></span>tar verification options:

- <span class="s1" style="font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-alternates: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-variant-position: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: normal;"></span>-d, --compare ,--diff —> Compares a tar archive file’s members with external files and lists the differences.
- <span class="s1" style="font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-alternates: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-variant-position: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: normal;"></span>-t, --list —> Displays a tar archive file’s contents.
- <span class="s1" style="font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-alternates: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-variant-position: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: normal;"></span>-W, --verify —> Verifies each file as the file is processed. This option cannot be used with the compression options.

- <span class="s1" style="font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-alternates: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-variant-position: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: normal;"></span>-x, —extract, —get —> Extracts files from a tarball or archive file and places them in the current working directory

- <span class="s1" style="font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-alternates: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-variant-position: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: normal;"></span>$ dd —> convert & copy a file

- <span class="s1" style="font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-alternates: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-variant-position: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: normal;"></span>$ ln —> make links between files

- <span class="s1" style="font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-alternates: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-variant-position: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: normal;"></span>$ ln -s —> soft link
- <span class="s1" style="font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-alternates: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-variant-position: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: normal;"></span>symbolic link / soft link: typically a soft link file provides a pointer to a file that may reside on another fs. being used for aliasing commands
- <span class="s1" style="font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-alternates: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-variant-position: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: normal;"></span>hard link: a file or dir that has one index (inode) number but at least two different filenames. it’s being used for protecting you from yourself specially when you are scripting
- <span class="s1" style="font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-alternates: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-variant-position: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: normal;"></span>notice: use $ unlink , when you want to delet a link, because it could be a security issue
- <span class="s1" style="font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-alternates: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-variant-position: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: normal;"></span>Version link:

- <span class="s1" style="font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-alternates: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-variant-position: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: normal;"></span>$ which java —> /usr/bin/java
- <span class="s1" style="font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-alternates: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-variant-position: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: normal;"></span>$ readlink -f /usr/bin/java —> /usr/lib/jvm/java-1.8.0-openjdk-1.8.0.201.b09-2.el7_6.x86_64/jre/bin/java

- <span class="s1" style="font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-alternates: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-variant-position: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: normal;"></span>$ readlink —> print resolved symbolic links or canonical file names

File Ownership

- <span class="s1" style="font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-alternates: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-variant-position: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: normal;"></span>three-tiered approach:

- <span class="s1" style="font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-alternates: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-variant-position: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: normal;"></span>Owner
- <span class="s1" style="font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-alternates: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-variant-position: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: normal;"></span>Group
- <span class="s1" style="font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-alternates: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-variant-position: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: normal;"></span>Others

- <span class="s1" style="font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-alternates: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-variant-position: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: normal;"></span>$ chown —> change file owner and group<span class="Apple-converted-space"> </span>

- <span class="s1" style="font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-alternates: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-variant-position: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: normal;"></span>$ chown NEWOWNER:NEWGROUP FILENAMES / or / $ chown :NEWGROUP FILENAMES

- <span class="s1" style="font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-alternates: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-variant-position: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: normal;"></span>$ chgrp —> change group ownership
- <span class="s1" style="font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-alternates: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-variant-position: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: normal;"></span>only root can change a file’s owner, only root or the owner can change a file’s group
- <span class="s1" style="font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-alternates: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-variant-position: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: normal;"></span>$ id -gn —> check your current group’s name
- <span class="s1" style="font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-alternates: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-variant-position: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: normal;"></span>$ newgrp groupname —> change your current group
